With regard  to nuclear weapons specifically, Russia reserves the right to use  nuclear weapons: in response to the use of nuclear and other types of  weapons of mass destruction against it or its allies,in case of  aggression against Russia with the use of conventional weapons when the  very existence of the state is threatened.   oops    google russia deadhand  The 'Perimeter' system, dubbed in the United States and Europe the 'Dead  Hand', is an automatic control system for a retaliation nuclear strike.  To put it simply, if Russia's territory is devastated after a nuclear  attack, the Perimeter system automatically strikes the enemy's territory  with its own nuclear missiles
